<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;

"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:BG'>Правописни правила<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:
3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#2D72B5'>Правопис на сложни
думи<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal'><span lang=BG style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:BG'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:
3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#917862'>Съществителни имена</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:#2D72B5'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><i><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:dimgray'>слято</span></u></i></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>&nbsp;се
пишат съществителните, при които</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>&nbsp;втората основа е
главна,&nbsp;<b>а първата я пояснява:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</b><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b>платно</b></span><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#917862'>ход</span></u></b><b><span

"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>ка</span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>&nbsp;(=&nbsp;<i>&nbsp;ход
чрез платно),</i>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b>ветро</b></span><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#917862'>показател</span></u></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>&nbsp;(=
показател чрез вятър)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><i><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

съществителните със&nbsp;</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:saddlebrown'>съчинително отношение&nbsp;<b>между двете
основи</b>:</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
покупко-продажба&nbsp;</span></b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:gray'>(покупка&nbsp;<b>и</b>&nbsp;продажба)</span></i><b><span

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;внос-износ&nbsp;</span></b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></i><b><u><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:red'>али</span><span

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Уподобяване на съгласните<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Представки,
които завършват на звучен съгласен, се пишат винаги с него независимо как се
изговарят:<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><strong><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2A87FF'>из,
без, през, раз, под, над, зад, пред, в, об</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:gray'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>При
изговор, ако след звучен съгласен има беззвучен, звучният се обеззвучава</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>проверка:</span><span class=apple-converted-space><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>хвърлям =<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span

color:gray'>+ хвърлям,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Променливо Я<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Пише се
и се изговаря -Я, когато:&nbsp;</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>1.)&nbsp;гласната е под ударение:</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;мл</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ко, сн</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>2.) следващата сричка НЕ съдържа</span></strong><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; мл</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Пише се
и се изговаря Я в множествено число на причастията на -Щ:</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;върв</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:brown'>ящ</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;– върв</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>ящи</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, сто</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:brown'>ящ</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;– сто</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>ящи</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, клон</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:brown'>ящ</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;– клон</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>ящи</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Подвижно Ъ (ър/ръ, ъл/лъ)<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Звукът
Ъ може да променя мястото си спрямо съгласните Р и Л!</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>В
едносричните думи липсва правило</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>стръв, грък, връх, глъч, плъх, плът<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>сърп, твърд, вълк, дълг, жълт, дърт<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>В
многосричните думи</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>1.) стои пред&nbsp;</span><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>Р</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;или&nbsp;</span><strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>Л</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, когато
след тях има само един съгласен звук:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>в</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ърб</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, г</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ърн</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>е, б</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ърк</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам, г</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ълч</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, м</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ълч</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>2.)&nbsp;</span><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>Ъ</span></strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;преминава след&nbsp;</span><strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>Р</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;или&nbsp;</span><strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>Л</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, когато
след тях има два или повече съгласни звука:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>В</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ръбн</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ица, г</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>рънч</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ар, б</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>рънк</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, г</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>лътн</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, мл</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ъкн</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ИЗКЛЮЧЕНИЕ</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;–
При глаголи от несвършен вид с наставка -</span><strong><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>В</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>-<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>изб</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ързв</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам, оп</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ържв</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам, прив</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ършв</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам, прет</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ърсв</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Изпадане на съгласни (елизия)<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Вътре в
думата само при изговор!</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p class=check style='background:#FAFAFA'><span class=check1><b><u><span
style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#5F8226'>проверка</span></u></b></span><span
class=check1><b><u><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:#5F8226'>:</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;чрез разлагане на думата на съставните
морфеми<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>властник = власт + ник, горестно = горест + но,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>тягостно = тягост + но, кръстци = кръст + ци,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>артистка = артист + ка, вестник = вест + ник<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ВНИМАНИЕ!</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>НЕ</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;се
пише съгласна -<strong><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>Т</span></strong>-
във формите на глаголите расна и пусна:</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>изра</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, прера</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, дора</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, пора</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>допу</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, пропу</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а, изпу</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>сн</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>а<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>-<strong><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>Т</span></strong>- се пише при
съответните глаголи от несвършен вид с наставка -<strong><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>В</span></strong>-</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>изра</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ств</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам,
прера</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ств</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам, дора</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ств</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам, пора</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ств</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>ам<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>В края
на думата съгласните изпадат само при изговор!</span><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p class=check style='background:#FAFAFA'><span class=check1><b><u><span
style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#5F8226'>проверка:</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;чрез
поставяне на думата в множествено число или членуване при имената от мъжки род<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>власт – влас</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ти</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, горест
– горес</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ти</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, артист
– артис</span><span class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>ти</span></u></b></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>, артист</span><span
class=bold-under><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ът</span></u></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Удвояване на съгласни (-ТТ-,
-ЗЗ-, -ДД-)<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>При
добавяне на представка, чийто краен звук съвпада с началния на корена</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>проверка:</span><span class=apple-converted-space><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>чрез разделяне
на представката от корена<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ОТ</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>-:<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>от</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Ітегля,<span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>от</span><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Ітласквам,<span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>от</span><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Іток,</span><span
class=apple-converted-space><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>&nbsp;</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>из</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>І</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>от</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>Ітатък,<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>от</span><span

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:gray;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
     auto;line-height:normal;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2;tab-stops:list .5in;

     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>намаляване
     на разстоянието между обекти:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
     font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
     mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;прикова, пришия<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:gray;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
     auto;line-height:normal;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2;tab-stops:list .5in;
     background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>еднократно
     или слабо действие:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
     "Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
     mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;пригърми, пришумоли, привали<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:gray;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
     auto;line-height:normal;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2;tab-stops:list .5in;
     background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>начало
     на действието:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;придреме
     ми се, прияде ми се<o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:
3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#2D72B5'>Представка О-
означава:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:gray;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
     auto;line-height:normal;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list .5in;
     background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>действието
     е върху повърхността на обекта:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
     font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
     mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;одраскам, ощавя, обеля<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:gray;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
     auto;line-height:normal;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list .5in;
     background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>действието
     е върху целия обект:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
     "Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
     mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;обера, ограбя, осоля, одирам<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:gray;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
     auto;line-height:normal;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list .5in;
     background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>за
     получаване на ново качество:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
     font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
     mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;оздравея, обогатя, облагородя,
     обуча<o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ul>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Представка У- означава:<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Действието
е към центъра на обекта</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>пример:</span><span class=apple-converted-space><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>убода,
ужиля<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Действието
е навън от центъра</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>пример:<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>улея,
убягна<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Действието
е надолу от центъра</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>пример:</span><span class=apple-converted-space><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>увисна,
упадна, утая<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Удвояване на предлозите В и С<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Kогато следващата
дума или цифра започва с<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><u>В/Ф</u><span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span>или<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><u>С/З</u>:</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>пример:<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>във
въздуха, във ІІ век след Хр.; със смях, със 7 години по-възрастен<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Когато
върху тях пада логическото ударение:</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>пример:<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Ще
замина със или без съгласието му.;&nbsp;Не знаем дали той е във или извън страната.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Краесловно обеззвучаване<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>При
изговор в края на думите звучните съгласни се обеззвучават, но&nbsp;</span><strong><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>винаги</span></u></strong><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;се
пишат звучните!</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>проверка:</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;- чрез промяна на думата в множествено число<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>гра</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>д</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– град</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ове</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, вло</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>г</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– влого</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ве</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, зали</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>в</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– зали</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ви</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>д</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>ди</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=check style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>проверка:</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;-
чрез членуване<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=check style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>гра</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:red'>д</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;–
гра</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>дът</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, вло</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>г</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– вло</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>гът</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, зали</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>в</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– зали</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>вът</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>д</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>дият</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=check style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>проверка:</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;-
чрез смяна на рода при прилагателните<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>бър</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>з</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– бър</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>за</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, бър</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>зо</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, благ – бла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>га</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, бла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>го</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>д</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;– мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>да</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>, мла</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:red'>до</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span lang=BG style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray;mso-ansi-language:BG'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span lang=BG style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:gray;mso-ansi-language:BG'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;
line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span lang=BG
style='font-size:20.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:BG'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;
line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span lang=BG
style='font-size:20.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:BG'>Граматични правила<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:
3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Особености на бройната форма<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><br
style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;mso-outline-level:4;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Особености
на бройната форма при съществителните имена &nbsp; от мъжки род<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><br>
- <b>Съществителните имена, назоваващи лица (мъже) имат само една форма за
множествено число, окончаваща на&nbsp;И:</b><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>двама
спортисти, пет инженери, осем войници, много ученици, малко учители<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>-
Съществителните имена за нелица имат различия при образуването на бройна форма:</span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>А)
при числителни те получават окончание&nbsp;А:</span></b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>пет
стола, седем чина, осем прозореца, девет компютъра, единадесет радиатора, два
бора<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Б)
при наречията за количество много, малко, толкова получават
окончание&nbsp;Иили&nbsp;ОВЕ:</span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>много
столове, малко чинове, толкова прозорци, много компютри, малко радиатори, много
борове<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:
3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Съгласуване на местоименията<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><br
style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;mso-outline-level:4;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Местоименията&nbsp;КОЙТО,&nbsp;КОИТО&nbsp;се
съгласуват с предходното съществително:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>*</span></b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>например:<b>&nbsp;</b>Бурята, която
счупи клоните на дъба, беше много силна.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;mso-outline-level:4;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Местоименията&nbsp;ЧИЙТО,&nbsp;ЧИИТО&nbsp;се
съгласуват със следходното съществително:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
line-height:normal;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>*</span></b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>например:<b>&nbsp;</b>Дъбът, чиито
клони са счупени…<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;
line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span lang=BG
style='font-size:20.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:BG'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;
line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:3;background:#FAFAFA'><b><span lang=BG
style='font-size:20.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:BG'>Пунктуация<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Подчинителни съюзи<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>Подчинителни съюзи:</span></strong><strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:saddlebrown'>&nbsp;</span></strong><span
class=apple-converted-space><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>който, чийто, какъвто;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>относителните местоименни наречия:&nbsp;</span></strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>където,
когато;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>подчинителните съюзи:</span></strong><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:brown'>&nbsp;</span></b></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>че, да;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:brown'>въпросителните местоимения и местоименни
наречия:</span></strong><span class=apple-converted-space><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>кой,
чий, какъв, кога, къде, как, защо, когато, докато, щом, след като, преди да,
защото, понеже, тъй като, въпреки че, макар че, затова., частицата дали и др.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Когато
подчиненото изречение е след главното изречение, запетая се поставя пред
подчинителния съюз или съюзна дума:</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Късните
студове тая зима се усилваха повече и повече от северните ветрове,</span></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>които</span></u></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>духаха
непрестанно от две недели насам.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Всички
се обърнаха в момента,</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>когато</span></u></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Бай
Ганьо спря един келнер, носещ поднос с кафета...</span></b></em><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br>
</span></i></b><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Имах чувството,</span></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>че</span></u></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>човекът
зад гърба ми се усмихва.</span></b></em><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br>
</span></i></b><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Малкото й &nbsp;личице бе мило и хубаво под
бялата забрадка,</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>чиито</span></u></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>краища
бяха пуснати свободно.</span></b></em><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br>
</span></i></b><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Враждата между двете страни достигаше
размери,</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>каквито</span></u></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>никога
не беше имала.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Запетая
се пише пред подчинено определително изречение, въведено чрез въпросителни
местоимения, наречия и частици:<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><u>кой,
чий, какъв, къде, кога, как, защо, дали и др</u>.:</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*</span></em><strong><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Даваха
му съвети,</span></i></strong><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><strong><i><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>какво</span></u></i></strong><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><strong><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>да
направи.&nbsp;</span></i></strong><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Ако
пред относителното местоимение който има предлог, запетая се пише &nbsp;пред
предлога:&nbsp;</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; *</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Тая
кръчма беше една дълбока изба,</span></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>в
която</span></u></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>се
слизаше по една стръмна и извита стълба.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:brown'>NB! Не се
пише</span></strong><span class=apple-converted-space><span style='font-size:
10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:brown'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:brown'>запетая
пред подчинителната съюзна дума<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><em><u><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>който (</span></u></em><strong><i><u><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>която, което, които</span></u></i></strong><em><u><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>)</span></u></em>, ако подчиненото
определително изречение не започва с нея, а с друга дума от състава си. В този
случай се поставя запетая пред началната дума в подчиненото изречение:&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Прокурорът
му зададе няколко въпроса,</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>смисълът
на които</span></u></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>беше
ясен...&nbsp;</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Не се
пише запетая пред еднократно употребен съюз<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><em><u><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>да,</span></u></em><span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span>служещ за връзка&nbsp; между
подчиненото определително изречение и главното:</span><span style='font-size:
10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; *</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>А
естествено аз нямам правото</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>да</span></u></b></em><em><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>бъда и
виновен.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>NB!</span></strong><span
class=apple-converted-space><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:#2D72B5'>&nbsp;</span></span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Когато подчиненото определително изречение,
въведено чрез съюза<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><em><u><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>да</span></u></em>, е след съчетание
от показателно местоимение и съществително име, се поставя&nbsp; запетая пред
да:</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<em><b><span style='font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif"'>*</span></b></em></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Тази
мисъл</span></u></b></em><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>,</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span

class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>помага
на бедните, го вълнуваше отдавна.&nbsp;</span></b></em><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Когато
подчиненото определително изречение е между частите на главното,&nbsp; се
огражда със запетаи и от двете страни:</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>На
същото небе<u>,</u></span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>върху

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><strong><span

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

дума, се отделя със запетая от следващото главно изречение:</span><span

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

или тире се поставя между обобщаващи думи и еднородни части, които ги

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>хляб,
свила, рози, нектар, цветя и плодове...</span></b></em><span style='font-size:

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></b></em><em><b><span

аз всичко тебе дадох</span></b></em><em><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>душа,
сърце, любов, зари небесни...</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*</span></b></em><em><b><span

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Вметнати думи и изрази<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![if !supportLineBreakNewLine]><br style='mso-special-character:line-break'>
<![endif]></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
"Times New Roman","serif"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:brown'>Вметнатите
думи и изрази</span><span class=apple-converted-space><span style='font-size:
10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:gray'>означават
увереност, предположение, последователност в излагането на мислите, лично или
чуждо мнение, обръщение, различни чувства, заключение. Вметнатите думи не са
свързани граматически с частите на изречението и при синтактичен разбор не се
подчертават.<o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Със
запетая се отделят следните вметнати думи и изрази: напротив, разбира се, от
една страна, от друга страна, първо, второ, трето, наистина, обръщенията
&nbsp;и др.:&nbsp;</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>Напротив</span></u></b></em><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>,</span></u></b></em><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>от тях
той почувства в душата си нещо пепеляво.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Работех</span></b></em><strong><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>,</span></strong><span
class=apple-converted-space><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></b></span><em><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>разбира се</span></u></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>...&nbsp;</span></b></em><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span

друга страна,</span></u></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>кога
сравним положението на работното население в американските градове с това в
Лондон, изведнъж се хвърля в очи благоденствието на първите и мизерията на
вторите. &nbsp;</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>*</span></b></em><em><b><span

class=apple-converted-space><b><i><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></u></i></b></span><em><b><u><span

той е богат човек</span></b></em><em><b><u><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></u></i></b></span><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>главата
му е гола като кратуна, а такива глави са много умни или много глупави</span></b></em><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>, и,

style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><span

той е народен представител.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:

за вас да гладувате...</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><strong><u><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Запетая
не се пише</span></u></strong><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:#2D72B5'>&nbsp;при следните вметнати думи и изрази:<span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><em><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>например,
всъщност, според мене, може би, за съжаление, следователно, вероятно, очевидно
и др.:&nbsp;</span></em></span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:

абсурдно.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

би</span></u></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><u><span

повярват на случката...</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

<p style='margin-left:.25in;background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:

съжаление</span></u></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span

казах аз.</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";

"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>&nbsp;</span></u></i></b></span><em><b><span

се връщаше нататъка...&nbsp;</span></b></em><span style='font-size:10.0pt;

<h4 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#2D72B5'>Вметнатият
израз може да бъде ограден със скоби, когато е с разширен състав и внася
странично пояснение:</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></h4>

<p style='background:#FAFAFA'><em><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana","sans-serif";color:green'>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*</span></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>Речта се
свърши при тържествена тишина</span></b></em><span class=apple-converted-space><b><i><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></span><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>(</span></u></b></em><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:#917862'>тогава
още не беше въведен обичаят на ръкопляскането</span></u></b></em><em><b><u><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>)</span></u></b></em><em><b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'>.&nbsp;</span></b></em><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana","sans-serif";color:gray'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:3.75pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:#FAFAFA'><span style='font-size:15.0pt;
